   document.addEventListener('turbolinks:load', function () {
      
    var urlOptions = {};
    if (returnTo) {
      urlOptions['return_to'] = returnTo;
    }
    var $ssoContainer = $("#social-sign-on-options, .sso_column");

    var appleCallbackUrl = "https://ifttt.com/auth/apple_id/callback";

    // deprecated: use data-action="link-apple-account" instead
    var $appleSignin = $('#appleid-signin');
    var appleSigninButtonHTML = $appleSignin.length && $appleSignin.get(0).innerHTML;
    if (appleSigninButtonHTML && Object.keys(urlOptions).length) {
      appleCallbackUrl += "?" + $.param(urlOptions);
    }

    $ssoContainer.on("click", "a[data-action=link-apple-account]", function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      window.App.Scripts.appleSSO(appleCallbackUrl, urlOptions);
    })

    window.App.googleAppKey = "427071021612.apps.googleusercontent.com";

    $ssoContainer.on("click", "a[data-action=link-google-account]", function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var googleCallbackUrl = "https://ifttt.com/auth/google_oauth2/callback";
      window.App.Scripts.googleSSO(googleCallbackUrl, urlOptions);
    });

    $ssoContainer.on("click", "a[data-action=link-facebook-account]", function(e) {

  <!-- Google Adwords Conversion Tags Support -->

    goog_snippet_vars = function() {
      var w = window;
      w.google_conversion_id = 955753877;
      w.google_conversion_label = "wpa6CO7ZjnEQlcvexwM";
      w.google_remarketing_only = false;

    goog_report_conversion = function(url) {
      goog_snippet_vars();
      window.google_conversion_format = "3";
      var opt = {};
      opt.onload_callback = function() {
        if (typeof(url) != 'undefined') {
          window.location = url;
        }
      }
      var conv_handler = window['google_trackConversion'];
      if (typeof(conv_handler) == 'function') {
        conv_handler(opt);
      }
    }
  /* ]]> */

  <!-- End Google Adwords Conversion Tags Support -->

    e.preventDefault();

  function setPageViewData() {
    window.App.pageViewData = (window.App.pageViewData || {});
    window.App.pageViewData.user_id = window.App.userId;
    window.App.pageViewData.session_id = window.App.browserSessionId;
    window.App.pageViewData.url = 'https://ifttt.com/?_hsenc=p2ANqtz-936bs2WiTeLExJ_SqRcjMBpb2AHqnsF7roUGbkwLvHoeC0kA22lgFunhQz8n2fSMPtezAW';
    window.App.pageViewData.path = '/';
    window.App.pageViewData.user_agent = window.navigator.userAgent;
    window.App.pageViewData.query_string = '_hsenc=p2ANqtz-936bs2WiTeLExJ_SqRcjMBpb2AHqnsF7roUGbkwLvHoeC0kA22lgFunhQz8n2fSMPtezAW';
    window.App.pageViewData.anon_id = '191a29d65d1021a7d0f0ac7ac9c6f6da';

    //array of controllers that have views that we don't want Segment to track
    window.App.denyList = ["passwords"]

    try {
      window.App.pageViewData.query_params = {"_hsenc":"p2ANqtz-936bs2WiTeLExJ_SqRcjMBpb2AHqnsF7roUGbkwLvHoeC0kA22lgFunhQz8n2fSMPtezAW"};
    } catch(e) {}

    window.App.pageViewData.hash = location.hash || '';
  }

  setPageViewData()

  function track() {
    var eventName = window.App.pageViewData.event_name || 'web.pageviewed';
    var denyEventList = ["web.pageviewed", "public_api.web_view.pageviewed"]
    if (denyEventList.includes(eventName)) {
      return
    }
    window.uiEventTracker.trackUserInteraction(eventName, window.App.pageViewData);
    window.uiEventTracker.trackPage(
      (window.App.pageViewData.path || eventName),
      window.App.pageViewData
    );

    delete window.App.pageViewData.event_name;
  }

  if(!window.App.denyList.includes('home')) {
    track()
  }

  document.addEventListener('turbolinks:visit', function() {
    window.App.pageViewData = {}
  }, { once: true });

    }, { once: true });

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var returnTo = "";

    window.fbAsyncInit = function () {
      FB.init({
        appId: '122259781154546',
        version: 'v2.9',
        cookie: true
      });
    }
    window.appleAsyncInit = function () {
      var appleButton = document.querySelector("#appleid-signin")
      var appleButtonHTML = appleButton && appleButton.innerHTML
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId: "com.ifttt.sso",
        scope: 'email',
        redirectURI: "https://ifttt.com/auth/apple_id/callback",
        state: "966cb8e91e5d39f3f505954b7245ea15",
        usePopup: true
      });
      if (appleButtonHTML) {
        // undo apple's automatic styling changes
        appleButton.innerHTML = appleButtonHTML;
      }
      if (appleButton) {
        document.addEventListener('AppleIDSignInOnSuccess', (data) => {
          var token = data.detail.authorization.id_token;
          window.location = "https://ifttt.com/auth/apple_id/callback?" + ("id_token=" + token) + (returnTo ? "&return_to=" + returnTo : "");
        });

        document.addEventListener('AppleIDSignInOnFailure', (error) => {
          window.appendFlash("Your Apple ID authentication failed.", "danger");
        });
      } // else we are using xhr AppleID.auth.signIn()
    }
    window.googleAsyncInit = function () {
      gapi.load('auth2', function() {});
    }
  </script>
  <script async="" defer="" onload="appleAsyncInit()" src="//appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js">
